<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preliminary_card">Preliminary card</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=UFC_140&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Preliminary card">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The first fight of the evening was between <a href="/wiki/Mitch_Clarke" title="Mitch Clarke">Mitch Clarke</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Cholish" title="John Cholish">John Cholish</a>. In the second round, Clarke attempted to take down Cholish. During the scramble, Cholish managed to take Clarke's back. Cholish flattened Clarke out and began striking Clarke until referee <a href="/wiki/John_McCarthy_(mixed_martial_arts)" class="mw-redirect" title="John McCarthy (mixed martial arts)">John McCarthy</a> stopped the fight.<sup id="cite_ref-USATodayPrelim_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-USATodayPrelim-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Cholish won the fight at 4:36 of the second round, due to a technical knockout, giving Clarke his first ever professional MMA loss.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Rich_Attonito" title="Rich Attonito">Rich Attonito</a> faced <a href="/wiki/Jake_Hecht" title="Jake Hecht">Jake Hecht</a> in the second bout of the night.
